<Name>begladwme</Name><date>1577042550345</date><rate>5<//rate>< Text>
I've been here many times!
So soothing, peaceful and wonderful.
A "foot massage"  starts with soaking your feet in warm water while they start massaging you from the head, neck,shoulders, and the arms, down to your hands!
Then you're nice warm feet get massaged including your calves up to your knees and then as an added bonus you turn over and they completely massage your back and neck and shoulders!!
This whole "foot massage" takes one whole hour!
I don't think that the workers make very much money by the hour so make sure you really tip them!
$10 or more.
Make a note of your favorite people so that you can ask for them by name when you come again! If you request somebody by name, you might want to tip them even more. My favorite, favorite people I tip at least $15 sometimes $20 if it is super unbelievabley fantastic!
and once you start to be known in there as a good tipper the massages which start out as fantastic, become out of this world!< /Text>

Orig review 8/'18, & revised review 8/'19 the same:
-- 3 Star service: Nothing stellar, but they are consistent and polite in getting the job done of relaxing the ol' body.
-- The great room containing 12 beds tends to be noisy with customers coming/going/talking/snoring, and the workers being heavy handed (noisy) with handling the foot-soak tubs and metal riser racks.
-- The workers also tend to sniffle (like a nasel drip) and throat clear throughout the entire massage. And, are heavy handed body work versus touching drop arm vs. setting it back on table.
-- 4 Star price: cash prepaid pack of 10 one-hour foot massages (in great room, but entire body with under clothes on gets done) is best way to go. Pay before service. Get what you pay for. Tip booklet given to patron post-service to leave cash tip--or, can give credit card at receptionist for tip.</text>

Friends and I came for happy hour. Cajun fries were delicious. The potato egg roll was interesting. It tasted like a smaller deep fried potato skin. The sauce was not ranch, but had a kick to it. The nachos were alright. It was topped with black beans, Pico, sour cream, and cheese. I won't order that again but I would try other things on their menu. My friend had their sliders and that looked good. Unfortunately, he didn't let me have a bite so I had to drool up close.

I didn't drink this time around, but my friends had more than one round of drinks so I assume it was good.

Maybe 5 TVs, with one game that has sound, inside the restaurant. And most importantly, the staff was friendly and attentative. A lot of things I liked about this place that I will be back.< /Review>

<review>Amazing, delicious burgers! Not too greasy, not too much sauce, pickles just the right thickness that and didn‚Äôt distract from the burger itself. I got mine without onion and looooooved it!!! My boyfriend got everything on his and said the onions were diced and were perfect amount of onion. We split an order of fries with cheese sauce on the side. I normally and not a fan of cheese sauce, but wow, this was so good! You can order the cheese sauce on the fries or in a cup on the side. I would recommend the cup so you can control how much cheese is on each fry when you dip, and then maybe save leftover cheese for chips at home. Splitting the fries with my bf was the perfect amount of fries for me, didn‚Äôt feel too full.

Also, Boylan sodas are so good! I got black cherry, and my bf got root beer. So good!

The staff was super friendly! And our order was ready way faster than they estimate, which is great. There‚Äôs parking behind and next to the building. We appreciate that all the packaging was paper, no plastic!< /review>< name>

Regular burger: pretty good. Two crispy smash patties w sauce and pickles. The flavor is great but it's missing that umphhh. Maybe more veggies?

Fries w cheese:
The fries are sooo good. The cheese sauce is alright; a bit too much for me. I got it on the side and am glad. I definitely have leftover cheese.

<rate>5<//rate>< Text>
A long overdue return to our favorite smash burger spot! The focused menu may be small but it's quality over quantity. The well seasoned ground beef patties are consistently juicy throughout and crisp at the edges, remaining true to the simplistic ethos of a smash burger. Simply finished with diced onions, ketchup, mustard, american cheese and some delightful sliced pickle. Ordering two is a no brainer. The fries might be the best I have tasted, fried in beef tallow which provides loads of flavor, it nostalgically reminds me of british chip shop chips. Wonderfully crisp and lightly salted their taste can hold their own if that is all you ordered. Paired with a cup of their in house cheese sauce it truly is a great flavor combo. Service is always warm friendly and Covid-conscious. It's a great experience that I wish I could do more frequently, enjoying top quality patties and fries off the warm hood of your car.</Text>

< Text>
A friend told me about this place a year ago and I've been meaning to get there for a while and we finally stopped by. It's delicious, just like everyone told me. I think what makes this place unique in today's food industry is it does the basics extremely well. They aren't trying to reinvent the burger, just make a simple burger tasty enough to not need to be loaded with ingredients that may or may not belong on a burger. I think the best way to describe it is a hand crafted McDonald's style burger but with the highest quality ingredients. The patty is a flavorful, crisp smashburger style that's still soft on the inside. The regular is a double and was the perfect size. I would even say fries are similar to McDonald's but a little thicker without the weird aftertaste or grease. The prices are fair and they have CVT soft serve. We will definitely be back soon.</Text>

1594216276272</Time>
< Rate>
5<//Rate>
< Text>
There's something about these burgers that I just can't explain. It's the purest and simplest burger you've ever ate, and I think the simplicity of it all brings out its true flavor. Their menu is also short and a sweet. They only serve burgers, fries and ice cream. They've added cookies and trinkets to the menu, but you know you're there for the burgers.

They come out with two flat patties, cheese, raw onion, ketchup, mustard and pickles. The patties are somewhat crispy which I find the be the whole charm of the place. It's a fun bite, and because of the lack of fancy condiments, it takes you back to more nostalgic times. It also reminds me of a McDonalds burger, except made to order!

Seating is all outdoors, and a few benches are found inside. They do have a small parking lot, but it does fill up quick. Street parking is available, just make sure to put enough time in your meters! This is no drive thru!

Keep in mind that because everything is fresh and made to order, the wait is usually out the door! You can't order ahead, so you have no choice but to wait approximately 30 minutes for your delicious burger!</Text>

It's a good burger. It has a charred taste, thin and has crunch when you bite it. With everything on it, it's a good one. I had my kids with me and I did a cheeseburger with a single patty and ketchup, and another single Patty and no added items. Both tasted great, with the plain one tasting like a summer backyard BBQ. The fries and soft serve were the hot for me as they complimented the whole taste. Perfect combo of salty and sweet to satisfy those two cravings. They do take credit card. The seating is limited and the order wait times are approximate. Friday @230pm the wait time for the order was 30 minutes, but ours came out faster even though it was 3 burgers, 3 fries and 2 soft serves.<//Review>

<review>This place is definitely worthy of all the praise it gets.  It is easily one of the best burgers I've ever had. It is a minimal masterpiece that will leave you wondering how such a simple burger can pack so much flavor. The way they make their patties is unique (as far as I know), they smash them until they are thin. This process results in a patty that has a unique, yet extremely satisfying texture and flavor. The edges of the burger have a delicious crisp to them. I could go on and on but just go check it out words cant describe this burger. Some tips tho: seating can be very limited so go ahead and eat in the parking lot or in your car, there is no shame in that and plenty do it. Things can add up quick here, keep costs down by ordering one order of fries per two people, they are very generous with fries here. Also they can triple or even quadruple stack the burgers if you ask!< /review>< Pics>
None</Pics>

< review>
There‚Äôs something about these burgers that I just can‚Äôt explain. It‚Äôs the purest and simplest burger you‚Äôve ever ate, and I think the simplicity of it all brings out its true flavor. Their menu is also short and a sweet. They only serve burgers, fries and ice cream. They‚Äôve added cookies and trinkets to the menu, but you know you‚Äôre there for the burgers.

They come out with two flat patties, cheese, raw onion, ketchup, mustard and pickles. The patties are somewhat crispy which I find the be the whole charm of the place. It‚Äôs a fun bite, and because of the lack of fancy condiments, it takes you back to more nostalgic times. It also reminds me of a McDonalds burger, except made to order!

Seating is all outdoors, and a few benches are found inside. They do have a small parking lot, but it does fill up quick. Street parking is available, just make sure to put enough time in your meters! This is no drive thr

Keep in mind that because everything is fresh and made to order, the wait is usually out the door! You can‚Äôt order ahead, so you have no choice but to wait approximately 30 minutes for your burger!<//review>

Thought 2:30 on a Saturday might be a good time to visit.  Was told there would be a half hour wait. Found instead it was a 45 min wait. Burgers are good, but not exceptional.  Slightly charred/crispy edge with a McDonalds Cheeseburger texture /flavor (soft flat burger mixed with melted cheese). Generous amount of fries (somewhere between In-N-Out and McDonalds - a good thing). Chocolate Ice Cream was the highlight - rich and flavorful. Nowhere to sit, so it had to all be consumed in the car.<//text>

<GmapID>0x80c2c748eebd79e5:0x35d71da5acdb75fa< /GmapID>< Review>
I've traveled around the world in search of the perfect burger, and let me tell you, this is as close to the Holy Grail as you can get. In terms of under $10, down and dirty, simple burgers, this is #1. The way the burger patties crunch and the American cheese oozes out, covering the entire mouth, alongside the punchy pickles and McDonald's style diced onions can only be described as an orgasm in the mouth. Perfect bun to meat to cheese ratios, great fries (close to McDonald's), and good people. Simple. Minimal. Tastes like nostalgia. Just remember, always order two.< /Review>

< Review>
Best burger ever. Drove from Las Vegas to have this amazing experience. Super friendly staff..< /Review>
< Gmap_id>
0x80c2c748eebd79e5:0x35d71da5acdb75fa<//Gmap_id>
</record>
</dataset><record>
<text>If McDonald's, sometime in the mid-80s, decided to beat In-N-Out at their own game, by paring their menu down to the bare essentials, while also focusing on elevating their minimalist cheeseburger to gourmet status (you know the one: thin patty, squirt of ketchup & mustard, micro-diced onions, neon yellow American cheese), you'd have Burgers Never Say Die (or BNSD for short).

"The Regular" is the name of the main event here: two thin patties ("smashed" in the local lingo, apparently to ensure the edges of the patty are perfectly crisp), gooey golden (not neon yellow) cheese slices, on a sponge-bread bun with just a hint of golden-brown toasting on the cut edges. Top it all off with the obligatory squirts of ketchup & mustard and a thin-sliced pickle or two, and you have a moment of near-perfect burger excellent that, alas, seems gone too quickly (perhaps I just ate it too fast).

Fortunately, the french fries are also approaching perfection. Served hot after being thin-cut and fried in beef tallow (McDonald's apparently only "flavors" them to taste like beef fat), one might even argue that they're worth a trip on their own.

Also very enjoyable is the soft-serve provided by CVT, in either chocolate, vanilla, or swirl. My disappointment that they didn't serve it to you in a cone quickly went away after tasting the first spoonful of swirl. The chocolate half is very reminiscent of Wendy's Frosty dessert, while the vanilla definitely has the edge over Mcdonald's soft-serve (although I'd still like to see a cone in the future).

My only complaint are the prices. Bring at least $20 for a burger/fries/drink/soft-serve meal. Ouch. I didn't mind so much after the first bite. Otherwise, it's a great new burger joint in L.A.

Recommended for both veggie-haters & meat-lovers.<//text>< Rate>
4< /Rate>

1565877218289<//date>

<rating>3</rating>< review>
BNSD is like chemotherapy; the results can be amazing but the process is painful, and longer than one would expect for a meal that only requires indirect heat.
